using \mbox{\hyperlink{paper_8txt_aa1f50b1f0bf1b6fe6599c279cf9ac25b}{line}} = ===============================================================================E\+L\+E\+M\+E\+N\+T\+A\+RY O\+P\+E\+R\+A\+T\+I\+O\+NS \mbox{\hyperlink{paper_8txt_a18d9a39516b037ef320c705fbd43f9e6}{L\+A\+LA}} works \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a29faf1efa547eee7395013df5586bda5}{with}} essentially only one kind of object, \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a19cefbe49a077540b7e33d4204e4b952}{a}} rectangular \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a87f6540bdacc78d66aa258ba9cb8419a}{matrix}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a29faf1efa547eee7395013df5586bda5}{with}} complex elements. If \mbox{\hyperlink{paper_8txt_a0e5a093c0749fb3ddf554bc9a3236a0f}{the}} imaginary parts of \mbox{\hyperlink{paper_8txt_a0e5a093c0749fb3ddf554bc9a3236a0f}{the}} elements \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ae2fdc33bcd49731e36913fa7258b0dc8}{are}} all zero, they \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ae2fdc33bcd49731e36913fa7258b0dc8}{are}} not \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a7a076662b7e84a2fa7ba1e6199ae1952}{printed}}, but they still occupy storage. In some situations, special meaning \mbox{\hyperlink{paper_8txt_abf86c805fff53b12fdd4129aff834228}{is}} attached to 1 \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a40eab2bd454e9f761f2d13dffa13fb19}{by}} 1 \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ab4a3112c11f40636a76f2bcc29d7cd3f}{matrices}}, that \mbox{\hyperlink{paper_8txt_abf86c805fff53b12fdd4129aff834228}{is}} scalars, \mbox{\hyperlink{paper_8txt_a9085509720f752e5fad3418387207221}{and}} to 1 \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a40eab2bd454e9f761f2d13dffa13fb19}{by}} \mbox{\hyperlink{paper_8txt_aeab71244afb687f16d8c4f5ee9d6ef0e}{n}} \mbox{\hyperlink{paper_8txt_a9085509720f752e5fad3418387207221}{and}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ab3cd915d758008bd19d0f2428fbb354a}{m}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a40eab2bd454e9f761f2d13dffa13fb19}{by}} 1 \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ab4a3112c11f40636a76f2bcc29d7cd3f}{matrices}}, that \mbox{\hyperlink{paper_8txt_abf86c805fff53b12fdd4129aff834228}{is}} row \mbox{\hyperlink{paper_8txt_a9085509720f752e5fad3418387207221}{and}} column vectors. Matrices can be introduced into \mbox{\hyperlink{paper_8txt_a18d9a39516b037ef320c705fbd43f9e6}{L\+A\+LA}} in four different ways\+:-\/-\/ Explicit list of elements, -\/-\/ Use of \char`\"{}for\char`\"{} and \char`\"{}while\char`\"{} statements, -\/-\/ Read from an external file, -\/-\/ Execute an external \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a0a890a7b5e140ce2ce94502357b159cf}{Fortran}} program. The explicit list \mbox{\hyperlink{paper_8txt_abf86c805fff53b12fdd4129aff834228}{is}} surrounded \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a40eab2bd454e9f761f2d13dffa13fb19}{by}} angle brackets, \textquotesingle{}$<$\textquotesingle{} \mbox{\hyperlink{paper_8txt_a9085509720f752e5fad3418387207221}{and}} \textquotesingle{}$>$\textquotesingle{} or braces \textquotesingle{}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{} \mbox{\hyperlink{paper_8txt_a9085509720f752e5fad3418387207221}{and}} \textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\textquotesingle{}, \mbox{\hyperlink{paper_8txt_a9085509720f752e5fad3418387207221}{and}} uses \mbox{\hyperlink{paper_8txt_a0e5a093c0749fb3ddf554bc9a3236a0f}{the}} semicolon \textquotesingle{}

\mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ac85e1322e210cd3e55055a318bee02d8}{as}} \mbox{\hyperlink{paper_8txt_a0e5a093c0749fb3ddf554bc9a3236a0f}{the}} singular \mbox{\hyperlink{paper_8txt_a6686ea9548b77078a675b45d345094b1}{value}} decomposition \mbox{\hyperlink{paper_8txt_a18d9a39516b037ef320c705fbd43f9e6}{L\+A\+LA}} should be useful in applied linear \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ac85e1322e210cd3e55055a318bee02d8}{as}} well \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ac85e1322e210cd3e55055a318bee02d8}{as}} more general numerical \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a87f6540bdacc78d66aa258ba9cb8419a}{matrix}} statistics \mbox{\hyperlink{paper_8txt_a9085509720f752e5fad3418387207221}{and}} \mbox{\hyperlink{paper_8txt_a6082ae76a6112377618cea922867233c}{applications}} of \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ab4a3112c11f40636a76f2bcc29d7cd3f}{matrices}} to other disciplines \mbox{\hyperlink{paper_8txt_a18d9a39516b037ef320c705fbd43f9e6}{L\+A\+LA}} can serve \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ac85e1322e210cd3e55055a318bee02d8}{as}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a19cefbe49a077540b7e33d4204e4b952}{a}} desk calculator \mbox{\hyperlink{paper_8txt_abf6b1e767d007146580c1e17b81f6196}{for}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ab4a3112c11f40636a76f2bcc29d7cd3f}{matrices}} The \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a352951c06b9686651e25162d794210a4}{program}} \mbox{\hyperlink{paper_8txt_abf86c805fff53b12fdd4129aff834228}{is}} written in \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a0a890a7b5e140ce2ce94502357b159cf}{Fortran}} \mbox{\hyperlink{paper_8txt_a9085509720f752e5fad3418387207221}{and}} \mbox{\hyperlink{paper_8txt_abf86c805fff53b12fdd4129aff834228}{is}} designed to be readily installed under any operating \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_af105eb2315d2a94fe1ffe3ce801ff395}{system}} which permits interactive execution of \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a0a890a7b5e140ce2ce94502357b159cf}{Fortran}} programs The \mbox{\hyperlink{paper_8txt_a8aa5df2f98d2a99467a113c196a6905e}{resources}} required \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ae2fdc33bcd49731e36913fa7258b0dc8}{are}} fairly modest The size of \mbox{\hyperlink{paper_8txt_a0e5a093c0749fb3ddf554bc9a3236a0f}{the}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ab4a3112c11f40636a76f2bcc29d7cd3f}{matrices}} that can be handled in \mbox{\hyperlink{paper_8txt_a18d9a39516b037ef320c705fbd43f9e6}{L\+A\+LA}} depends upon \mbox{\hyperlink{paper_8txt_a0e5a093c0749fb3ddf554bc9a3236a0f}{the}} amount of storage available on \mbox{\hyperlink{paper_8txt_a18d9a39516b037ef320c705fbd43f9e6}{L\+A\+LA}} resembles S\+P\+E\+A\+K\+E\+A\+SY\mbox{[}4\mbox{]} to \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a19cefbe49a077540b7e33d4204e4b952}{a}} lesser A\+PL All \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ae2fdc33bcd49731e36913fa7258b0dc8}{are}} interactive \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a38e6d74dbec5d98dd45386bba314f0b6}{terminal}} languages that ordinarily \mbox{\hyperlink{paper_8txt_abdb34322ff76ea8e7365a03da7d4167e}{A}} equals the number of rows of \mbox{\hyperlink{paper_8txt_ad3a46ad317f8826946f3c9a3ea39acc7}{B}} \mbox{\hyperlink{paper_8txt_a9085509720f752e5fad3418387207221}{and}} the number of columns of \mbox{\hyperlink{paper_8txt_abdb34322ff76ea8e7365a03da7d4167e}{A}} plus the number of columns of \mbox{\hyperlink{paper_8txt_ad3a46ad317f8826946f3c9a3ea39acc7}{B}} equals the number of columns of \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a3a063ab18ff9fbeff794f149723fdd91}{C}} This rule generalizes in \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a19cefbe49a077540b7e33d4204e4b952}{a}} hopefully obvious \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a50bb17654285ab47c528bd15c11e15ce}{way}} to allow fairly complicated constructions
